# FECLedger — Test Cases
*Manual browser checklist. Run locally: `python3 -m http.server 8080` from project root.*

---

## How to use this file

**Automated tests (Track 1):** Run `npx playwright test` from the project root before and after changes. 811 structural tests across all pages run in ~2.6 minutes with mocked API. See `TESTING.md` for full details.

**Smoke tests (Track 2):** Run `npm run test:smoke` before deploys. Hits the live FEC API — 5 key checks. Requires the dev server to be running.

**Manual browser checks:** Use the checklists below for things automated tests can't verify — visual design quality, chart rendering, animation smoothness, content accuracy. Run for every page touched in a session. **Local dev:** `npm run dev` → http://127.0.0.1:8788/ (Cloudflare-parity, runs Pages Functions). Do NOT use `python3 -m http.server` — it cannot run the API proxy and broke silently on 2026-04-14.

**Amplitude verification method:** Open DevTools → Network tab → filter for `api2.amplitude.com`. Each event appears as a POST request. Click the request to inspect the payload and confirm event name + required properties. `Page Viewed` should fire within 2 seconds of load. Interaction events should fire only on user action, not on programmatic init calls.

**Checkboxes reset each session** — uncheck everything before starting a run. The Test log is the persistent record, not the checkboxes.

## How to maintain this file

- **New feature lands:** Add test cases in the same session it ships. New page = new section. New feature on existing page = new cases in that section.
- **Known issue resolved:** Remove from Known open issues table; add corresponding test cases to the page section.
- **Scaffold → live transition:** Expand that page's section from scaffold-scope to full coverage.
- **Test log:** Append a row for every test run. Never delete old rows — they show the testing history.

---

## Shared — run for every page touched this session

*Items marked ✅ are covered by automated tests (`npx playwright test`). Run manual checks for the rest.*

- [ ] ✅ `styles.css` and `main.js` both linked
- [ ] ✅ Top nav present with 2 main nav links (Races, Feed)
- [ ] ✅ Mobile search toggle present
- [ ] ✅ Page background is warm parchment (not dark or white)
- [ ] ✅ Amplitude `Page Viewed` fires on load
- [ ] ✅ No uncaught JS errors on load
- [ ] Page loads without console errors (open DevTools — automated checks miss network/CORS noise)
- [ ] Light broadsheet theme applied — visually warm parchment, not dark or white
- [ ] Oswald used for headings and display text
- [ ] IBM Plex Sans used for body and nav text
- [ ] IBM Plex Mono used for data labels and monospaced values
- [ ] Top nav visible and fixed at both desktop and mobile widths
- [ ] At ≤860px: nav links hidden, hamburger and search toggle visible; mobile nav drawer drops down on hamburger click
- [ ] At ≤860px: search toggle expands inline search panel below nav; closes when hamburger drawer opens and vice versa
- [ ] At ≤860px: mobile nav drawer and search panel appear *below* the nav bar and *above* all page content including sticky profile headers (z-index check)
- [ ] At ≤860px: mobile nav drawer does not partially overlap or sit behind the top nav bar (DOM structure: both panels are children of `.top-nav`, `position:absolute; top:100%`)
- [ ] At ≥861px: full nav links and search bar visible; mobile controls hidden
- [ ] Nav links resolve: Races → /races, Feed → /feed (Candidates + Committees retired from top nav 2026-05-20 — reached via search "View all" or direct URL)
- [ ] Global search bar (desktop): submits to /search?q=…
- [ ] Amplitude: `Page Viewed` fires within 2 seconds of load (verify via Network tab → api2.amplitude.com)

### Tooltip surfaces (info-icon ⓘ tooltips, 2026-06-01) — candidate + committee

*Component behavior (hover/click/keyboard/Esc/outside-click/scroll-close, popup placement, singleton) is covered by `tests/tooltip.spec.js`. These check the per-surface application — placement, copy, and no-layout-impact.*

- [ ] ✅ Donut legend wedges (Raised tab): the 6 methodology wedges each show a ⓘ; popup shows the wedge's copy; legend rows are even (no row grows — `.donut-row` is 32px)
- [ ] ✅ Choropleth title (Raised tab): "Itemized Individual Contributions Map" has a ⓘ; popup = geography + amendment caveat (both pages, identical copy)
- [ ] ✅ Spending by Purpose title (Spent tab): ⓘ; popup = "Categories estimated…miscategorized" + a single trailing parenthetical combining the conditional clauses: "(covers {YYYY}–{YYYY} only, capped at 500 transactions)" / "(covers {YYYY}–{YYYY} only)" / "(capped at 500 transactions)" / none. The "covers …" clause is candidate multi-sub-cycle only (House omits; committee omits — cap-only)
- [ ] ✅ Candidate Top Vendors title shows the last sub-cycle's date range — "Top Vendors · {YYYY}–{YYYY}" (e.g. 2023–2024), mirroring committee; never the static "Most Recent Sub-Cycle" (retired 2026-06-11). House: range = the cycle; Senate/President: the last 2-year window of the cycle
- [ ] ✅ Future election cycle (e.g. a 2028 Senate incumbent viewed in 2026 — `/candidate/S0GA00559#2028`): the page fully loads (map, Spending by Purpose, Top Contributors, Top Vendors all resolve — not stuck in skeleton; timeline plots the filed periods). `/committees/?cycle={future}` is empty, so the principal resolves via the unscoped-committees fallback. Opex (Vendors + Purpose) scopes to the most-recent FILED sub-cycle (e.g. "Top Vendors · 2025–2026" + "Covers 2025–2026 only."), NOT the empty nominal last (2027–2028). Top Contributors does NOT error: the slow tier skips the future sub-cycle (its `two_year_transaction_period={future}` Schedule A query 404s) by capping at the filed period
- [ ] ✅ Archive divider (index view, pre-threshold cycles only): ⓘ on the "Archived …" band; popup = "No detail view available for … prior to {threshold}"; band stays 32px (doesn't grow)
- [ ] ✅ Raised:Spent ratio stat label (candidate, detail view): ⓘ in the card's top-right corner; popup = "Total receipts ÷ total disbursements"; **card and stats-grid row do NOT change height** (the `.tooltip` host is `position:absolute`; the trigger button inside is `position:static`)
- [ ] ✅ Tooltip aria-labels are sentence case (first word capitalized, rest lowercase except proper/product terms): "About candidate authorized committees", "About other receipts", "About spending by purpose", "About the Raised:Spent ratio"
- [ ] At ≤860px: each ⓘ remains tappable; popup opens and clamps inside the viewport (≥8px from both edges); no horizontal page overflow
- [ ] Spent footer (`#spent-data-note`) is empty/hidden; Raised footer (`#raised-data-note`) shows only the conduit explanation (the cut source/scope/vendor notes are gone)

- [ ] Cycle index column headers: Cycle / Raised / Spent / Cash on Hand

- [ ] index→detail with compact engaged: header visibly compact immediately on detail load — no tall-to-compact flicker

- [ ] index compact → click cycle row → scroll detail UP (un-compacting it) → back: index still compact; detail's un-compact state didn't leak
- [ ] Gillibrand: cycle rows grouped by election (e.g. "2019–2024" for a 6-year cycle), not by individual sub-cycle

- [ ] Profile menu-btn → Committees item in index view opens the committees modal normally

### Raised/Spent loading + error states (T12 + T12.5)
- [ ] Mock 429 on `/schedules/schedule_a/?is_individual=false` (DevTools Network → custom response) → click Raised → tab-error UI on slow tier with rate-limit copy ("⚠ FEC API rate limit reached. Please wait a minute, then reload the page."); no retry button
- [ ] Mock 500 on same endpoint → click Raised → tab-error UI with default copy + retry button visible; clicking retry re-fires the fetch
- [ ] Mock 429 on `/candidate/{id}/committees/?cycle=2024` (init-stage failure) → both Raised + Spent tabs show tab-error UI with rate-limit copy when clicked; no retry buttons; no skeletons hold forever
- [ ] Mock 500 on same endpoint → both Raised + Spent show init-failure copy ("⚠ Couldn't load this page. Please reload to try again.")
- [ ] Slow-tier `/schedules/schedule_a/?is_individual=false` fetch in flight at 10s → "still loading…" augmentation appears under the slow-tier skeleton
- [ ] Cycle switch after tab-error → error states clear, fresh fetch attempted

### Spent tab loading + error states

## search.html

**Test URL:** `localhost:8080/search.html`

### Amplitude events
- [ ] `Page Viewed` fires with `page: 'search'`
- [ ] `Candidate Searched` fires on search submit with `query` property
- [ ] `Candidate Result Clicked` fires on candidate card click with `candidate_id`, `candidate_name`, `query`, `result_position`
- [ ] `Committee Result Clicked` fires on committee row click with `committee_id`, `query`, `result_position`

### Live inline results
*(T-search-inline-results — the floating typeahead dropdown was retired; /search renders live results in the page body via `initSearchPanel`.)*
- [ ] Typing 1–2 characters → nothing appears below the search bar — no results, no error screen (the FEC API rejects keyword queries shorter than 3 characters, so the panel fires no fetch below 3 chars)
- [ ] Typing 3+ characters → results render inline in the page body within ~350ms (no floating dropdown)
- [ ] Results show a "Candidates" group and a "Committees" group, each with a count header
- [ ] Refining the query (typing more) keeps the prior results visible — no flash to a blank/loading state
- [ ] During an in-flight refine, a thin accent progress bar shows along the top edge of the results region
- [ ] Clicking a candidate card navigates to `/candidate/{id}` (clean URL)
- [ ] Clicking a committee row navigates to `/committee/{id}` (clean URL)
- [ ] Pressing Enter pushes `/search?q={query}` to the URL; results stay visible (no re-fetch flash, no blank)
- [ ] Clearing the input back below 3 characters hides the results

### Results display
- [ ] Each group header reads e.g. "5 candidates for "cantwell"" with count first, label second, query in quotes
- [ ] Candidate cards link to `/candidate/{id}` (clean URL, no `?id=`)
- [ ] Committee rows link to `/committee/{id}` (clean URL)
- [ ] Candidate card shows name (First Last), race tag, latest-cycle tag, party tag
- [ ] Committee row shows name, committee type, Active/Terminated status tag
- [ ] If total candidates > 5: "View all N →" link appears and links to `/candidates?q={query}`
- [ ] If total committees > 5: "View all N →" link appears and links to `/committees?q={query}`
- [ ] "View all" links absent when count ≤ 5
- [ ] If both groups return 0 results: no-results state shown (not blank)
- [ ] If the FEC API fails: error state with a Retry button shown (not blank)
- [ ] `localhost:8080/search.html?q=pelosi` auto-fires search on load and shows two-group results
- [ ] Cold query (first search, no prior results visible) shows the centered loading spinner

- [ ] localStorage keys prefixed `lf:race:{cycle}:{office}:{state}:{district}` visible in DevTools → Application → localStorage
- [ ] At-large House seats (WY, AK, MT) display without district suffix (e.g. "House • WY" not "House • WY-00")
- [ ] Changing office or state filter updates results instantly with no API call; observer re-fires for newly visible rows
- [ ] Changing cycle triggers new API fetch, full re-render with skeletons, and observer re-wires
- [ ] Filter chips appear for active office and state filters (not cycle)
- [ ] Clearing a chip resets that filter and re-renders
- [ ] "Clear all" button appears when 2+ chips active
- [ ] No-results state shown when filters match zero races
- [ ] Error state shown on API failure; retry button re-fetches
- [ ] Races sorted by state then district within each office group

### URL sync
- [ ] Applying Office or State filter updates the URL (e.g. `/races?cycle=2026&office=H&state=WA`)
- [ ] Changing cycle updates URL with new cycle value
- [ ] Loading `/races?cycle=2024&office=S` restores those filters on page load (cycle dropdown set, office select set, results filtered)
- [ ] Loading `/races?state=WA` restores state filter (state combo input + listbox value set)
- [ ] Clearing all filters resets URL to `/races?cycle=XXXX` (cycle always present)

### Results area
- [ ] `#state-results`, `#state-loading`, `#state-no-results`, `#state-error` all present ✅
- [ ] Retry button present in error state ✅

## race.html

**Test URL:** `localhost:8080/race.html?state=WA&district=03&year=2024&office=H`
*(2024 is a completed cycle with known filings — 2026 is too early to have reliable financial data)*

### Amplitude events
- [ ] `Page Viewed` fires with `page: 'race'` and `state`, `year`, `office`, `district` properties
- [ ] `Candidate Result Clicked` fires on card click with `candidate_id`, `from_page: 'race'`, `race_year`

### API correctness
- [ ] No 422 error in console (confirms office param is sent as lowercase full word: "house", not "H")
- [ ] Check Network tab: the `/elections/` API call includes `office=house` (not `office=H`)

### Header template (shared with candidate.html and committee.html)
- [ ] Header uses `.page-header` wrapper — same padding and border-bottom as candidate and committee headers
- [ ] Race title uses `.page-title` — same Oswald 600, clamp(2rem,5vw,4.5rem), uppercase
- [ ] Header fades in on load (opacity transition via `.page-header-reveal`)

### Race header (de-tabbed — T-remove-profile-tabs race final pass, 2026-06-04)
- [ ] Race title reads "US HOUSE: WASHINGTON'S 3RD DISTRICT" (long-form, uppercase via `.page-title`)
- [ ] Browser tab title reads "US House: Washington's 3rd District — FECLedger"
- [ ] No tabs bar — the candidate list IS the page (single flowing content; Insights stub deferred to Phase 4)
- [ ] Year dropdown is inside `#race-header` (controls cluster), right-aligned (T-move-race-year-select, 2026-06-03)
- [ ] Year dropdown + seat-class cluster top-aligns to the title row; seat-class stays vertically centered with the dropdown
- [ ] Scroll into compact header: year dropdown stays visible + un-stretched (~34px), right-aligned in the slim strip
- [ ] No candidate count in header or meta (removed)
- [ ] ✅ Year dropdown shows 2024 as selected value when URL param is `year=2024`
- [ ] Candidate list renders directly (no tab to click); the Insights stub was removed (Phase 4 will re-add it as a flowing section)

### In-place cycle switching (T-race-inplace-cycle, 2026-06-03 — no full reload)
- [ ] Changing the year dropdown updates the candidate list, count, and `?year=` **without a full page reload** (no white flash / scroll-to-top jump)
- [ ] URL `?year=` updates on each switch (pushState); browser Back returns to the prior cycle in place; Forward re-applies
- [ ] Switch while scrolled into the compact header on a same/longer cycle → scroll position + compact header preserved (no jump)
- [ ] Switch from a long cycle to a much shorter / empty one → page settles to ~top, the compact header expands (animated, not a hard jump)
- [ ] Senate race: switching cycles updates the seat-class (e.g. PA 2024 "Class I seat" → 2022 "Class III seat")
- [ ] Switch to a cycle with no candidates → inline empty state ("No candidates found…"), not a blank void and not the full-page loader
- [ ] During a switch a brief centered spinner shows; the prior list doesn't collapse underneath it
- [ ] Failed switch (kill network on the `/elections/` call) → inline error above the list, **prior cycle's list stays intact + usable**, dropdown snaps back, `?year=` unchanged; Retry re-loads the cycle that failed
- [ ] Bare URL (`/race?state=WA&office=H&district=03`, no `?year=`) → URL canonicalizes to `?year={resolved}` (replaceState; Back still goes to the referrer, not a self-loop)
- [ ] Amplitude: initial load fires `Page Viewed { trigger: 'load' }`; each cycle switch (dropdown or back/forward) fires `Page Viewed { trigger: 'cycle-switch', year }` — the two are distinguishable in analytics (race has no `view` field like candidate/committee)

### Candidate-card refinements (T-race-page-UI, 2026-06-03 — race.html only)
- [ ] "Candidates (N)" label is the larger Oswald 1.25rem treatment (`.raised-cell-title`), not the small mono label
- [ ] Desktop: each card's name is on the left, the 3 stats (Raised / Spent / Cash on Hand) sit **side-by-side on the right**, vertically centered, **right-aligned**
- [ ] Desktop: the same stat lines up in a column **across stacked cards** (Raised under Raised, etc.) — values right-edge aligned
- [ ] No divider line between name and stats (the old top-border was retired)
- [ ] ≤860px: name and stats **stack** (stats below the name), **left-aligned**, in even thirds; no horizontal overflow
- [ ] A candidate with no financial activity ($0/$0, the live API shape) shows **"No financial activity reported"** (muted body text) in the stats slot — in BOTH desktop (right side) and mobile (stacked) layouts
- [ ] A presidential-scale value renders as billions (e.g. `$1.5B`, not `$1500.0M`) and fits the stat column without clipping
- [ ] **No regression on shared surfaces:** `/candidates` and `/search` candidate cards are unchanged (still 16px 8px padding, no side-by-side stats) — the changes are scoped under `#race-list`

### Page-level data note — RETIRED (2026-06-01)
- [ ] ✅ `#race-note` is NOT present in the DOM (element + populating JS removed entirely; automated regression-lock in pages.spec.js). race.html isn't yet rich enough to warrant a page-level data note — deliberate divergence from candidate.html / committee.html, which keep `#page-note`.

### Dynamic cycle dropdown
- [ ] ✅ Year dropdown options populated from `/elections/search/` endpoint (not hardcoded)
- [ ] House race: dropdown shows historical cycles from FEC data, capped at current cycle
- [ ] Senate race: dropdown shows cycles for both seats (unioned), capped at current cycle + 4
- [ ] No future projected cycles beyond the cap (e.g. no 2060)
- [ ] Network tab: `/elections/search/` and `/elections/` fire near-simultaneously (parallel fetch)
- [ ] If `/elections/search/` fails: dropdown falls back to [2026, 2024, 2022, 2020, 2018]; console warning fires
- [ ] Year in URL not in dropdown (e.g. `year=2028` with no data): page snaps to nearest valid cycle

- [ ] ✅ House race does NOT show class label (`.race-seat-class:empty` → no stray gap beside the dropdown)

- [ ] Switching year on Senate race: class label updates correctly on reload
- [ ] Class label uses caption type role (IBM Plex Mono 400 · 0.625rem), `--muted` color (T-move-race-year-select restyle, 2026-06-03)

### URL param validation
- [ ] ✅ Invalid state (e.g. `state=ZZ`) shows error with back link to /races
- [ ] ✅ Invalid office (e.g. `office=X`) shows error
- [ ] ✅ Odd year (e.g. `year=2023`) shows error
- [ ] Garbage params (e.g. `state=ABCDEFG`) show error, not a loading spinner
- [ ] Valid but no-data params (e.g. `state=WY&office=S&year=2024`) show "No candidates found" (not error)

- [ ] State combo: selecting from listbox populates text input and triggers fetch
- [ ] Office combo: clicking trigger opens custom listbox; selecting "President" disables state filter; selecting other option re-enables it; trigger label updates
- [ ] Party combo: clicking trigger opens listbox; selecting a party re-fetches and updates trigger label

- [ ] Clicking chip `×` clears that filter and re-fetches
- [ ] "Clear all" chip appears when 2+ filters active; clears everything and re-fetches
- [ ] ✅ URL updates (pushState) after every filter change — `?office=H`, `?state=WA`, etc.

- [ ] ✅ Error state (`#state-error`) renders and retry button visible when API fails

*(T-search-typeahead-retire — the live filter-field typeahead was retired; /candidates is enter-to-search.)*

- [ ] Typing 1–2 characters then Enter falls back to browse mode — no error, header/chips read as "showing all" (not `for "<query>"`); the FEC API rejects keyword queries < 3 chars
- [ ] Network tab at 0/1/2/3 chars: no `/api/fec/` request carries a `q=` value shorter than 3 characters

## Pre-deploy checks — clean URL pages

*Run before committing any changes to `candidate.html`, `committee.html`, or `race.html`, or when adding a new profile page. Playwright cannot catch this class of bug.*

- [ ] `styles.css` linked as `href="/styles.css"` (absolute), not `href="styles.css"` (relative)
- [ ] `main.js` linked as `src="/main.js"` (absolute)
- [ ] `utils.js` linked as `src="/utils.js"` (absolute)
- [ ] All nav links use absolute paths: `/candidates`, `/committees`, `/races`, `/search`, `/`, `/process-log.html`, `/design-system.html`
- [ ] Any outgoing links to other profile pages use clean URL format: `/candidate/{id}`, `/committee/{id}`
- [ ] race.html: sidebar logo links to `/` (not `index.html`); all nav items use `/candidates`, `/committees`, etc.

## Post-deploy checks (Netlify only — cannot run locally)

*These verify clean URL rewrites in `_redirects`. Run against `sloanestradley.netlify.app` after any deploy.*

- [ ] `/search` loads search.html (not 404)
- [ ] `/candidates` loads candidates.html (not 404)
- [ ] `/committees` loads committees.html (not 404)
- [ ] `/races` loads races.html (not 404)
- [ ] `/candidate/H2WA03217` loads candidate.html with MGP's profile (not 404 or blank)
- [ ] `/committee/C00744946` loads committee.html with committee data (not 404 or blank)
- [ ] `/race?state=WA&district=03&year=2024&office=H` loads race.html with candidate cards (not 404 or blank)
- [ ] Browser URL bar shows clean path (not `.html` equivalent) for all above
- [ ] Navigating to a clean URL and refreshing does not 404

| 2026-04-21 | Session 4B — cm.txt (FEC Committee Master File) integration: data-layer-only, no HTML/CSS/JS changes. Up-front verification against the FEC description page and a real cm26.txt confirmed 15 columns, pipe-delimited, no header row, LF-terminated, pure ASCII — plus two quirks found before any code: (a) literal `"` chars embedded mid-field in CMTE_NM (e.g. `CONSTANCE "CONNIE" JOHNSON`) — fix: DuckDB read_csv with `quote=''`, not the default `quote='"'`; (b) no header row in the source — handled by prepending `CMTE_ID\|CMTE_NM\n` at ingest (via BulkProcessingStream) and reading with `skip=1`. (1) ingest-bulk.js: added `cm22`/`cm24`/`cm26` to FILES (pipeline now processes 9 files); new `CM_HEADER` + `CM_KEEP_COLS = [0,1]` constants; replaced `isIndiv` boolean dispatch with `fileConfig()` helper (per-type switch on url/r2Key/header/keepArr) shared between `processFile()` and `main()` HEAD-request URLs; last_updated.json write extended to `{ indiv, pas2, cm }`. Atomicity contract preserved: the existing `allSucceeded` gate in the for-loop automatically covers cm failures, so any cm file failing skips the whole last_updated.json write for that run. (2) precompute-aggregations.js: added `CM_COLUMNS` schema (2 cols); cm.csv downloaded per cycle alongside pas2+indiv; `buildCommitteesAggSql(pas2Path, cmPath)` rewritten with a `committee_names` CTE and two LEFT JOINs (`cn_g` on giver, `cn_r` on receiver) — display name is `COALESCE(cn_g.name, upper(trim(f.name)))` (cm.txt registered name primary, pas2 filer NAME fallback for unregistered givers), self-affiliate filter compares cm-sourced names on both sides (lenient on NULL); ID-level filter kept as belt-and-suspenders; cleanup `fsp.unlink(cmPath)` at cycle close. `ENABLE_TOP_COMMITTEES_PASS` flipped to `true`. | 2026-04-21 | Historical backfill (1980–2020) + precompute skip logic: data-layer-only, no HTML/CSS/JS changes. Research-verified (via HEAD-check + column-count smoke on real 1980/1990/2000/2010/2014/2020 samples) that all three FEC bulk file types exist at the standard URL pattern from 1980 onward with stable schemas (indiv=21 cols, pas2=22 cols, cm=15 cols), 404 at 1978 and earlier, no format blockers. (1) ingest-bulk.js: `FILES` array extended from 9 to 72 entries (3 types × 24 cycles 1980–2026). (2) precompute-aggregations.js: `CYCLES` extended from 2 to 24 (1980–2026 including the 2022 gap-fill). (3) Global `wipeNamespace()` at pipeline start replaced with per-cycle `wipeCycleKeys(cycle)` inside the main loop — lists the full namespace and filters client-side by `:${cycle}` suffix before bulk-delete. This makes skipping cycles safe (their KV data stays) and means a partial-run failure doesn't wipe untouched data. (4) Precompute skip logic: new nested `state.precompute` object in `fec/meta/pipeline_state.json` storing per-cycle `{indiv, pas2, cm}` Last-Modified tuples captured at each successful precompute. At the top of `processCycle`, compare the current ingest-side tuple (from flat `state[${type}${yy}]` keys written by ingest) against `state.precompute[year]`; skip the cycle's SQL + KV work if all three match. Also skip (with a distinct log line) if any ingest-side key is missing — avoids SQL against non-existent R2 objects. (5) `main()` loop now writes `state.precompute[year]` to R2 after each successful cycle (wipe + KV write succeeded), mirroring ingest's per-file write-on-success pattern — a mid-run failure at cycle N doesn't re-do cycles 1..N-1 on retry. (6) Local DuckDB smoke test against sampled 1990 pas2 + cm confirmed `buildCommitteesAggSql()` runs cleanly on historical data with sparse ENTITY_TP. (7) **Execution took 3 bug-fix commits past initial**: (a) `parallel=false` on read_csv for pas2/indiv — DuckDB's parallel scanner fails on `null_padding=true` + quoted-newline fields (modern FEC data has multi-line OCCUPATION/EMPLOYER strings from 2012+); caught on 2022 indiv line 8,755,603. (b) `strict_mode=false` + `ignore_errors=true` — historical indiv/pas2 rows contain literal `"` inside field content (`"K" LINE AMERICA INC`, `"GRAMMIES" FOR BARTON`, `"S" ATTORNEY`, etc.) that aren't CSV-quoted; same class as cm.txt's embedded quotes but can't use `quote=''` since modern data DOES have legitimate CSV-quoted fields. (c) `memory_limit='8GB'` (up from 4GB) + `SET preserve_insertion_order=false` — 2020 indiv is 9.6 GB (largest in dataset), OOMed at 4GB. | 2026-04-23–24 | **T6.5 — In-place index↔detail transitions + compact header continuity.** Replaced `window.location.reload()` hashchange handler with persistent `switchView()` function: profile header stays stable during cycle-row clicks and browser back/forward; only below-header content swaps. Key mechanisms: (1) `switchView(true/false, cycle)` — shows/hides index/detail elements via `display` + `classList.add/remove('visible')`; fires Amplitude `Page Viewed` on each call; owns scroll management. (2) Fetch-race token: `currentFetchId` counter incremented at `loadCycle()` top, checked after each async phase — stale in-flight calls discard DOM writes. (3) Data cache: `cachedHistory`/`cachedAllTotals` set on first index fetch, reused on back-navigation → zero re-fetch. (4) `history.scrollRestoration = 'manual'` prevents browser auto-scroll on hashchange. (5) Tab hash captured before `await loadCycle()` — `loadCycle()` calls `replaceState(#cycle#summary)` internally, overwriting the original `#cycle#raised` before we can read it. (6) Cycle switcher populated unconditionally in `init()` before view-branching. (7) Compact header continuity: `compactThreshold` exposed from `initCompactHeader()` as a module var; `switchView(true)` scrolls to threshold (not 0) when `indexScrollY >= compactThreshold`; `switchView(false)` never touches compact class — scroll listener is sole owner. `initCompactHeader()` called unconditionally in `init()` so compact works on index-only visits. (8) `minHeight` fix: detail view in skeleton state is shorter than viewport; `scrollTo(compactThreshold)` was clamped to 0 by browser. Fix: set temporary `.main` minHeight before the scrollTo, clear after `loadCycle()` populates real content. 10 new Playwright tests in a `candidate.html — in-place transitions` describe block; scroll-behavior tests use `page.evaluate(() => { window.location.hash = '...' })` instead of `element.click()` — Playwright's click() auto-scrolls into view, resetting scrollY before switchView() can read it. | candidate.html, tests/candidate.spec.js, CLAUDE.md, TESTING.md, test-cases.md | Manual verification caught 3 bugs after initial Playwright-green implementation: (1) compact not working on index-only visits (`initCompactHeader` was only called in switchView detail branch — moved to init()); (2) scroll restoration clamped on back→index (renderIndexFromData called before display:block; moved render before RAF, scrollTo inside RAF); (3) scrollTo(threshold) clamped to 0 (document shorter than viewport in skeleton state — minHeight fix). Strategy doc `strategy/t11-5-conduit-gate.md` banks the analysis. CLAUDE.md got the `memo_code=X silently ignored` API-quirk note. No production code changes. **T12 (`f496351`) — progressive Raised + Spent loading states:** rescoped from the original "lazy fetch" plan after latency investigation showed `/schedules/schedule_a/?is_individual=false` page-1 takes 5–25s for principal CCs (cold cache). Real lazy fetch was decided to be blocked on KV pipeline extension to top-committees + top-conduits; T12 rescoped to loading-state polish only. `fetchRaisedData` split into `fetchRaisedFastData` (by_state, sub-second) + `fetchRaisedSlowData` (Schedule A non-indiv pagination). Donut renders synchronously from totals (in memory). Per-tier skeleton + per-tier error UI with retry. 10s "still loading" augmentation via `setTimeout` keyed on fetch start, fires globally regardless of which tab is visible. Spent tab keeps single-tier shape. Inner try/catch removed from Spent fetches so errors propagate to the tab-error UI. New CSS: `.tab-skeleton` block variants (skeleton-donut/map/table/bars), `.tab-still-loading`, `.tab-error` + `.tab-retry-btn`. **T12.5 (`ef377d0`) — 429-aware tab-error + init-stage failure bridging:** `is429(err)` detector + `TAB_ERROR_RATE_LIMIT_MSG` + `TAB_ERROR_INIT_FAILURE_MSG` constants in utils.js. `showTabError(errorEl, err, defaultMsg)` helper inline on each profile page picks the variant (default → retry button; 429 → no retry, "wait a minute, reload"; init-stage → no retry, "reload to recover"). `loadCycle()` outer catch on candidate.html bridges to set `raisedFastError = raisedSlowError = spentError = err` (with `err.initStage = true`) and calls render functions so the tab-error UI surfaces — without bridging, kickoffs sat after the awaited init calls that threw and skeletons held forever. **Donut skeleton (`ba1eee8`):** added `#raised-donut-skeleton` + `#raised-donut-content` toggle on Raised tab so the donut cell shows a skeleton during cycle-switch and cold-load instead of an empty canvas. **Skeleton refactor (`506480a`):** all chart/table cells consolidated to title-always-visible pattern — section title (`.raised-cell-title`, `.donors-head`) renders immediately; only the chart canvas / table body area swaps between skeleton and content. Removed unified `#spent-skeleton-wrap` + `#spent-content` two-state toggle on Spent tab; replaced with per-section skeletons. Removed `border-bottom` from `.donors-head`. **Contributions polish (`c1add5a`):** committee.html Spent → "Contributions to Candidates & Committees" — data note moved below the table; whole-row link via absolute `::before` overlay (native `<a>` semantics: middle-click, keyboard, screen reader). | 2026-04-28 | **T9 + T10 + 4 verification fixes — committee.html parity arc closes (in-place transitions).** Six commits this session. **T9 (`8ec232b`):** Lifted candidate.html's `switchView()` into `initViewSwitcher(config)` factory in `utils.js` (~110 lines). Diagnosed via inline `console.log` instrumentation in initViewSwitcher + tiny one-off Playwright spec capturing values across both pages. Cause: helper cleared minHeight after loadCycle resolved, assuming natural content had grown — true for candidate's async loadCycle (awaits totals fetches), false for committee's sync wrap (Promise.resolve(renderStats)). Fix: don't clear minHeight at all. The minHeight is a harmless floor when natural content exceeds it (raised/spent tab switches) and necessary when natural is short (committee skeleton state). Conditional clear-then-restore tried first and failed — the momentary clear is enough to trigger browser-side clamping. Test scaffolding upgraded: switched committee in-place compact test from `body.minHeight=3000px` (which masked the bug) to inflating `cycle-index` padding only (the realistic flow). Migrated candidate.spec.js's analogous test to the same pattern in the post-verification ritual. **Verification fix 2 (`c31d58d`) — trailing slash on committee URL:** `/committee/{id}/` returned the "No committee specified" error state because `.split('/').pop()` returns `''` for trailing slashes. Fixed by switching to `.split('/').filter(Boolean)` then taking the last segment — exact same pattern candidate.html had since T5/T6. 4 new tests on each spec file (no-slash + trailing-slash for both pages). **Verification fix 3 (`71236a0`) — regression-parity sweep across no-ID + non-existent year + invalid tab:** Sloane's prompt asked for parity verification of three more candidate-era patterns. Three of four checks confirmed clean. Same pattern existed on committee.html. Fixed both pages by excluding the clean-URL page name from the ID guard. Plus committee's no-ID friendly message updated to link to /committees (was just suggestion text). 4 new tests on each spec file (no-ID friendly state on both URL forms, non-existent year fallback, invalid tab hash normalization). | candidate.html, committee.html, utils.js, tests/candidate.spec.js, tests/committee.spec.js, CLAUDE.md, ia.md, TESTING.md, test-cases.md, claude-to-claude.md | Workflow lesson banked: end-of-session rituals run AFTER verification, not bundled with implementation. | 2026-05-20 | **T-load-header-title-skeleton — Profile-header name skeleton renders during load.** Diagnosed an exists-but-broken latent bug from the T-load-1 work: both candidate.html and committee.html ship `<span class="skeleton" style="width:60%;height:1em">` inside `#candidate-name` / `#committee-name` (verified in source at line 107 / 105), but the spans render at zero width. Empirical probe via Playwright `getBoundingClientRect`: name skeleton `width: 0px, height: 64px`; parent `.page-title` also `width: 0px`; meta-row skeleton works fine at `473px × 19px`. **Root cause:** the `width:60%` percentage references the parent's resolved width, but `.page-title` is a flex item inside `.profile-header-row` (a flex container) with no explicit `width`/`flex-basis`/`flex-grow` — only `min-width:0`. So `.page-title` sizes to its content; the content IS the skeleton; the skeleton's percentage references the parent's resolved width, which depends on its content. Circular ref → CSS spec resolves to 0. The meta-row's 40% works because `.meta-row` is a block-level sibling of `.profile-header-row` (a direct child of `.page-header`), not a flex item itself — its width is determined by `.page-header`'s content area, so percentage references resolve cleanly. **Fix:** changed both name-skeleton width values from `60%` to `8em` — em scales with the parent's clamped font-size (`2rem`–`4.5rem`), so width ranges 256–576px across viewport widths, landing roughly 60–80% of typical resolved title widths in Oswald 600 condensed uppercase. Matches the existing `height:1em` em-based pattern, and matches T-load-3's absolute-unit approach (ch widths for stat-grid skeletons) — same family of fix for the same class of percentage-vs-flex-item gotcha. **Tests:** +2 (591 → 593). One per page in the existing T-load-1 describe block — asserts the skeleton renders at `width > 100px` and `height > 20px` during a 2000ms entity-fetch delay window (specifically catches the zero-width regression). **Docs touched:** CLAUDE.md ("Skeleton profile-header (T-load-1)" paragraph updated with the new 8em width + banked gotcha note about percentages inside flex items), TESTING.md (test count 591→593 + describe-block updates on both spec files), test-cases.md (this row). **No strategy doc** — investigation was Playwright-probe-driven and small; the gotcha banked in CLAUDE.md is the durable artifact. | candidate.html, committee.html, tests/candidate.spec.js, tests/committee.spec.js, CLAUDE.md, TESTING.md, test-cases.md | Live verification recommended on `fecledgerapp.pages.dev` after deploy: (a) `/candidate.html?id=H2WA03217` cold load (DevTools "Disable cache", Slow 3G throttling) — name skeleton visible during the entity-fetch window alongside the meta-row skeleton; resolves to "Marie Gluesenkamp Perez" when entity lands; (b) `/committee/C00775668` same — name skeleton visible during load; resolves to real committee name; (c) mobile viewport (≤860px) — name skeleton sized appropriately (8em × 1em scales down with clamped font-size); (d) very narrow viewport — skeleton doesn't wrap or overflow. | 593/593 Track 1 passing (+2 net: was 591) |
| 2026-05-20 | **T-committee-init-defer-totals — Per-path totals await on committee.html init().** Banked follow-up from T-load-4a, scoped by `strategy/committee-init-scaffold.md` (diagnostic written before implementation). **Cross-page convention is the load-bearing win, not latency.** Before: committee.html init() awaited entity then totals before view.switchTo (eager init-level totals await); candidate.html init() awaited only entity, totals fired per-path. After: both pages share the same init() invariant — **init() awaits only entity; totals is per-path.** **Implementation:** `await totalsP` moved into `if (isDetailView)` branch (detail view needs ALL_TOTALS sync for renderStats); a `totalsP.then()` populator at init() sets `ALL_TOTALS` as soon as totals resolves AND re-fires `renderStats(activeCycle)` if the user clicked a cycle row before totals landed; `.catch(swallow)` on the populator (helper's onPartialError surfaces real failures). Empty-ALL_TOTALS guard added at top of `renderStats` — short-circuits cleanly, leaving T-load-3 skeletons in place until the populator re-fires. Re-fire guard: `activeCycle && document.getElementById('summary-strip').style.display !== 'none'` — verified that (a) `#summary-strip` is toggled exclusively by inline `el.style.display` in utils.js's `initViewSwitcher` helper (no class-based hide path), and (b) `activeCycle` is null on index path (only set inside `renderStats` which only runs from the helper's `loadCycle` callback in the detail branch). **Honest payoff:** modest. On warm-cache loads (typical for repeat visitors), saves ~0–500ms of scaffold visibility. On worst observed cold-cache cases from T-load-1 measurements (43s entity, 14s totals), entity is slower than totals → today's await was already a no-op → refactor saves 0ms there. The win is most visible when totals happens to be slower than entity. Strategy doc made this trade explicit. **Tests:** +3 (588 → 591). Cycle-index scaffold renders independent of /totals/ (1500ms delay; scaffold visible <1500ms; career raised/spent cells still skeletoned during await window; hydrate after delay); cycle-row click during /totals/ load shows stat skeletons until totals resolves, then renderStats re-fires via totalsP.then() populator and #stat-raised hydrates to real value; detail-URL cold load still awaits totals before view.switchTo (no dashed stats from empty ALL_TOTALS — regression-locks the conditional await on the detail path). **Docs touched:** CLAUDE.md (existing "Committee.html init() flow note" rewritten to describe new per-path pattern + cross-page invariant + banked follow-up marked shipped), TESTING.md (test count 588→591 + describe-block update on committee.spec.js), test-cases.md (this row), strategy/committee-init-scaffold.md (EXECUTED banner in follow-up commit). | committee.html, tests/committee.spec.js, CLAUDE.md, TESTING.md, test-cases.md, strategy/committee-init-scaffold.md | Live verification recommended on `fecledgerapp.pages.dev` after deploy: (a) `/committee/C00580100` bare URL cold load (DevTools "Disable cache") — career-strip + cycle-index visible from first paint; financial cells skeletoned during /totals/ window; hydrate progressively after /totals/ resolves; (b) `/committee/C00580100#2024#summary` cold load — stat cells skeletoned during loading window, resolve to real values when totals lands (NOT dashes from empty ALL_TOTALS — that would indicate init didn't await on detail path); (c) cycle-row click during a delayed /totals/ load (use DevTools throttling to make totals slow enough) — click cycle row immediately after page loads but before totals resolves; stat cells should hold skeleton placeholders, then hydrate to real values when totals lands; (d) back navigation (detail→index) — cycle-index renders from cached promise without refire; (e) committees with deep history (e.g. Gillibrand PCC) — scaffold visibility most pronounced on slow connections. | 2026-05-19 | **T-loadcycle-single-fetch — Simplify loadCycle to election_full=true single fetch.** Banked from T-load-4a follow-ups. Today's loadCycle iterates subcycles and sums client-side: 1 call for House (already optimal), 2 for Presidential (cycle-2 + cycle), 3 for Senate (cycle-4 + cycle-2 + cycle). Replaced with a single `/candidate/{id}/totals/?cycle={cycle}&election_full=true` call returning FEC's pre-aggregated record. Largest network-call reduction on Senate cold-cache detail loads (3 calls → 1). **Data parity verified live across H/S/P samples on 2026-05-19** before the swap: Gillibrand 2024 ($15.72M receipts, $25.32M disb, $715K COH, 2024-12-31 covEnd — identical between approaches), Trump 2024 ($3.85M / $831K / $0 / 2024-08-08 — identical), Marie 2024 ($11.86M / $11.90M / $26K — identical). COH and coverage_end_date on the election_full record represent end-of-cycle values, semantically aligned with the prior "most-recent subcycle" treatment. Breakdown fields (13 receipt + 5 disbursement categories used by the donut chart) all FEC-aggregated and identical to client-side sum. Debt fields (loans_received + debts_owed_by_committee) verified parity across 6 candidates including non-zero-spend losing campaigns (Beto O'Rourke 2018, Hillary 2016, Cori Bush 2024) — both approaches produce identical values; the field is typically null/0 on candidate-totals records regardless of actual end-of-cycle debt status, but parity holds. **Edge case probed:** Trump 1988 (election_year present but no /totals/ election_full record) returns `{results: []}` cleanly from both query variants; new code's `(fetchResults[1].results || [])[0] || {}` guard handles identically to today's iterate-and-sum catch path. **Implementation:** ~30 fewer LOC in loadCycle Step 1. | 2026-05-21 | **T-search-inline-results follow-up — FEC API 3-char keyword minimum.** Live verification of the shipped Phase 1 work surfaced a threshold bug: a 2-character query (e.g. "ma") fired a fetch the FEC API rejects (keyword queries must be ≥3 chars), surfacing the `#state-error` "COULDN'T LOAD RESULTS" screen for what is just the API's minimum-length rule. `initSearchPanel`'s `query(q)` guard was `< 2` — off by one. Fix: renamed `MIN_CHARS` → `MIN_QUERY_LENGTH`, value 2 → 3, with a WHY comment (FEC rejects <3-char keywords; do not lower). | 2026-05-28 | **T-meta-row-column arc (3 commits — try / revert / restructure).** **First commit (39e4d17, T-meta-row-width):** added `max-width:max-content` to `.meta-row` to size it to its tags' natural width (~294px) instead of stretching to fill the page-header content area. | 2026-05-29 | **T-tooltip-component — designed info-icon tooltip + design-system entry.** Replaces the project's browser-default `title`-attribute pattern with a markup-driven info-icon tooltip component. Author writes `<span class="tooltip" aria-label="...">trusted-HTML content</span>`; `initTooltips(rootEl?)` in utils.js wires every `.tooltip` host into a 32×32 `<button class="tooltip-trigger">` (with Material Symbols `info` outlined/filled icon variants in `var(--accent)` color) and lazily creates a `role="tooltip"` popup portaled to `document.body` on first reveal. Portal-to-body is required because consumer surfaces (chart cards, donut labels, vendor tables) carry `overflow:hidden` ancestors that would clip inline popups. **Positioning:** popup top edge contiguous with trigger bottom edge (zero gap per Figma); vertical flip-above when no room below; horizontal clamp to 8px inside both viewport edges. Custom vanilla-JS positioning, not Floating UI — matches project no-build convention. **Interaction:** hover with 100ms reveal delay (0ms under prefers-reduced-motion); combined hover region with 100ms hover-handoff close timer; click tap-toggle; Tab + Enter via keyboard; Escape closes + returns focus; outside pointerdown closes; scroll/resize close (rAF-deferred listener attachment guards against in-flight scroll from the click gesture). **Singleton** — only one popup open at a time. **Filled-iff-revealed** icon rule with preemptive `:focus-visible:not(:hover)` Safari sticky-focus-on-tap guard. **A11y:** trigger has aria-haspopup/aria-expanded/aria-label/aria-describedby; popup has role="tooltip"; missing aria-label → console.warn + skip wire; nested `<button>` ancestor → console.warn + proceed. AbortController-based listener teardown (second codebase consumer after openAccessibleModal). New utility helpers `info` + `info_filled` added to `ICON_PATHS` (Material Symbols 400, Apache 2.0). **Tests:** new tests/tooltip.spec.js with 20 tests covering aria contract, hover/click/tap-toggle/keyboard, escape, outside-click, singleton, scroll/resize, flip-above, horizontal-shift, reduced-motion, missing-label + nested-button warnings. **Docs:** CLAUDE.md `initTooltips` entry under Shared files (with full API + a11y + positioning); design-system.html new comp-tooltip card with two live demos (short content + ~47-word stress case with link). Status: stable from day one (shared component, intended for all 3 profile pages downstream). | utils.js, styles.css, design-system.html, tests/tooltip.spec.js, CLAUDE.md | Consumer-side application is downstream (V1 TOOLTIP-VIZ / TOOLTIP-LABEL rows in strategy/data-notes-mapping-v2.md §1). | 680/680 Track 1 passing (+20 net: was 660) |
